Aviva_NNP plc_NN 89_CD Accounts_NNPS and_CC notes_VBZ Notes_NNS to_TO the_DT accounts_NNS continued_VBD 38_CD Long-term_JJ business_NN provision_NN a_DT Methodology_NNP There_EX are_VBP two_CD main_JJ methods_NNS of_IN actuarial_JJ valuation_NN of_IN liabilities_NNS arising_VBG under_IN long-term_JJ insurance_NN contracts_NNS the_DT net_JJ premium_NN method_NN and_CC the_DT gross_JJ premium_NN method_NN both_DT of_IN which_WDT involve_VBP the_DT discounting_NN of_IN projected_VBN premiums_NNS and_CC claims_NNS ._.
Under_IN the_DT net_JJ premium_NN method_NN ,_, the_DT premium_NN taken_VBN into_IN account_NN in_IN calculating_VBG the_DT provision_NN is_VBZ determined_VBN actuarially_RB ,_, based_VBN on_IN the_DT valuation_NN assumptions_NNS regarding_VBG discount_NN rates_NNS ,_, mortality_NN and_CC disability_NN ._.

This_DT method_NN does_VBZ not_RB allow_VB for_IN voluntary_JJ early_JJ termination_NN of_IN the_DT contract_NN by_IN the_DT policyholder_NN ,_, and_CC so_IN no_DT assumption_NN is_VBZ required_VBN for_IN persistency_NN ._.

However_RB ,_, this_DT method_NN makes_VBZ implicit_JJ allowance_NN for_IN future_JJ regular_JJ or_CC terminal_JJ bonuses_NNS already_RB earned_VBN ,_, by_IN margins_NNS in_IN the_DT valuation_NN discount_NN rate_NN used_VBN ._.
The_DT gross_JJ premium_NN method_NN uses_VBZ the_DT amount_NN of_IN contractual_JJ premiums_NNS payable_JJ and_CC includes_VBZ explicit_JJ assumptions_NNS for_IN interest_NN and_CC discount_NN rates_NNS ,_, mortality_NN and_CC morbidity_NN ,_, persistency_NN and_CC future_NN expenses_NNS ._.

Explicit_JJ provision_NN is_VBZ made_VBN for_IN vested_JJ bonuses_NNS and_CC explicit_JJ allowance_NN is_VBZ also_RB made_VBN for_IN future_JJ regular_JJ bonuses_NNS ,_, but_CC not_RB terminal_JJ bonuses_NNS ._.

The_DT principal_JJ assumptions_NNS in_IN the_DT United_NNP Kingdom_NNP ,_, France_NNP and_CC the_DT Netherlands_NNPS are_VBP :_: i_FW United_NNP Kingdom_NNP The_DT net_JJ premium_NN method_NN is_VBZ used_VBN for_IN most_JJS contracts_NNS except_IN term_NN assurances_NNS in_IN the_DT Norwich_NNP Union_NNP Life_NNP &_CC Pensions_NNP and_CC Norwich_NNP Union_NNP Linked_NNP Life_NNP funds_NNS ,_, business_NN in_IN the_DT with-profit_NN funds_NNS of_IN CGNU_NNP Life_NNP and_CC Commercial_NNP Union_NNP Life_NNP ,_, and_CC non-profit_JJ deferred_VBN annuity_NN and_CC with-profit_NN business_NN in_IN the_DT Provident_NNP Mutual_NNP Fund_NNP ._.
For_IN term_NN assurances_NNS in_IN the_DT Norwich_NNP Union_NNP Life_NNP &_CC Pensions_NNP and_CC Norwich_NNP Union_NNP Linked_NNP Life_NNP funds_NNS ,_, business_NN in_IN the_DT with-profit_NN funds_NNS of_IN CGNU_NNP Life_NNP and_CC Commercial_NNP Union_NNP Life_NNP ,_, and_CC non-profit_JJ deferred_VBN annuity_NN and_CC with-profit_NN business_NN in_IN the_DT Provident_NNP Mutual_NNP Fund_NNP ,_, the_DT provisions_NNS are_VBP valued_VBN using_VBG the_DT gross_JJ premium_NN method_NN ._.

This_DT result_NN is_VBZ then_RB compared_VBN with_IN a_DT prospective_JJ valuation_NN and_CC the_DT higher_JJR result_NN is_VBZ taken_VBN ._.
The_DT prospective_JJ valuation_NN projects_NNS future_JJ benefits_NNS on_IN the_DT assumption_NN that_IN future_JJ premiums_NNS cease_VBP and_CC regular_JJ bonuses_NNS are_VBP decreased_VBN to_TO the_DT guaranteed_VBN rate_NN or_CC nil_NN ,_, at_IN a_DT rate_NN consistent_JJ with_IN policyholder_NN reasonable_JJ expectations_NNS ._.
